 is bill menmanav taskarise nipatane ke liye sakht praavdhaan kiye gaye hai or aise maamalon kaa nipataara tay samay ke andar kiya jayega

 log in rajdhani dilli ke patpadganj main ek mandir ban rahaa he
 If this thing was so, then there is no need to write, because temples continue to be built all over the country
 magar ye mandir sarkari zamin par ban rahaa he
 In most places, temples or mosques are seen on government land
 kuch log paksh main hote hai or kuch vipaksh main virodh karne waalon kii aawaaj aksar ansuni kar di jaati he
 The issue is that near the plot number 44 of Patparganj, people of the Kripal Society are building a temple on land that does not belong to them
 haalanki unka daawa he ye ki unki jameen he or vah is par jo chaahe kar sakate hai
 But people outside the society have become cautious about this, fearing that this temple being built illegally should not cause tension
 pichley kuch dinon se ye mandir achaanak kripal sosayadi se lagi sarkari zamin par banane laga he
 When we reached this society of Patparganj in East Delhi, many types of questions were asked to us, who told us that a temple is being built here
 unka kahana he ki yahaan purana mandir tha or ve use phir se banavaa rahe hai
 He was also denying that this is the land of DDA i
e
 Delhi Development Authority
 unka kahana tha tees saal se vah jameen unki castady main he or tab to didie ne is par koi aawaaj nahin uthaai or ab ham jo chahen so karen
 People were even telling us that how did you come here and ask whom
 philhal yahaan tak pahunchane kaa bas ek hi rasta he jo socity ke get se hokar hi jaataa he
 Later it was discovered that there was another way to reach here, which was stopped by the society
 jab ham sosayadi se baahar ke logon se mili to unka kahana he ki yah zamin sarkari he
 The Kripal Society has wrongly captured it
 in logon ko mandir ke banane se etraz nahin he
 There are complaints about occupation of government land
 is baat se bhi ki yahaan aane jane ke raste ko socity waalon ne kyon band karavaaya
 When the DDA officials were talked about in this regard, they also admitted that an illegal temple is being built on government land and a complaint has been made to the Delhi Police to stop its construction, but no concrete action has been taken so far
 is
 vahiin police kaa tark he ki abhi vah trilokapuri main hue dangon ko rokane lagi he, baad main ise dekhegi
 Meanwhile, the construction work of the temple is going on in full swing
 isse sate ilaake main jhuggi bhi he, jahaan har samudaay ke log rahete hai
 Talking to people revealed similar stories which often become a dose during times of stress
 ek reporter ke taur par mujhe laga ki aakhir dilli main trilokapuri yaa duusare rajyon main tanaav to choti hi baat se shuru hua or baad main jab aag bhadki to us par kaabo paanaa kaaphi mushkil ho gaya
 By the way, this place is just one and a half kilometers from Trilokpuri and it does not take time for the spark to spread
 pichley saal sadakon par dharmik sthalon ke nirmaan par roak lagate hue supreme court ne kaha tha ki saarvajanik sadak kisi kii sampatti nahin he
 Everyone has the right to go through the road and it cannot be stopped or obstructed by building a temple, mosque, church or gurudwara or statue of a big figure
 saal 2008 main maujuuda pradhanmantri or tab gujarat ke mukhyamantri rahe narendra modi ne ahmedabad main sadak main padane vaale 90 aise dharmik sthal hatwa die the, jinamein zyaadaatar mandir the
 The question is whether his government will ban the roads or religious places built in government places in Delhi too
 teji se vikaas kii seedhi chadhane vaale gudgaanv ke ek sarkari college main students toilet main baithkar padhane ko majaboor hai
 Toilets have been made temporary for the last two years due to lack of classroom at Dronacharya Government College located on New Railway Road
 college ke toilet main eme soshiyology kii class chalati hai
 On this, the principal of the college, RK Yadav says that he is short of government funds and due to this he is not able to get a class
 unke mutabik, 'hamen kam se kam 25 classroom kii jarurat he
 Last year, the government approved to build 12 classrooms, but funds for construction work have not yet been received
 'vahiin student kaa kahana he ki new arts block ke toilet main baithkar class karnaa apmanjanak to he, lekin dhoop main baithne se to behatar he
 He says that the college administration had told him last year that new classrooms would be built within a year, but nothing has happened so far
 yahi nahin class ke dauraan toilet se aane vaali badboo se bhi student pareshaan hai
 Although the toilet is cleaned cleanly, there is no relief
 ve is baat se bhi dukhi hai ki duusare college ke student unhen toilet main padhai karne kii vajah se bahut chidhaate hai
